  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_51869bd1-ca2f-48fe-bc29-d883b2a09007'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);
    };

      initAppleId();
    } else {
      initializeSiwa();

<div id="descriptionContainer">
  
      <div id="description" class="readable stacked" style="right:0">
        
<span id="freeTextContainer10093668467478205055">Enter into the enchanting world of the Mystic Warriors. Where an ageless immortal society of gifted and powerful supernatural beings exist, unknown to man, with magic and the ability to control the elements of nature and use these ability to fight the forces of darkness. Desire, love, and adventure lie ahead for two unlikely souls destined to be together.<br/>Powerful shifter, </span>
  <span id="freeText10093668467478205055" style="display:none">Enter into the enchanting world of the Mystic Warriors. Where an ageless immortal society of gifted and powerful supernatural beings exist, unknown to man, with magic and the ability to control the elements of nature and use these ability to fight the forces of darkness. Desire, love, and adventure lie ahead for two unlikely souls destined to be together.<br />Powerful shifter, telepath and practitioner of magic, Bly La Croix is a true daughter of the earth. She’s a descendant from a long line of Elemental warriors and magical beings as a protector of mankind while living among normal man as one of them. The various roles she’s assumed over time afforded her the secrecy necessary to fulfill her protective role to man. <br />Andrew Von Erikson, the eldest of the Von Erikson triplets born over six hundred years ago. The situation surrounding their birth created the one of a kind warrior that they are. Known to the society of Elementals as Day Walkers, they are a triple threat to combat the evil of the world. Due to the circumstance of his birth Andrew exists in a world of isolation, expecting nothing, to never find a mate who can save him from the shadows that haunt his being. <br />They were both summoned to return to Nos Ysse Kraggenra – Sanctuary Mountain, by the governing council of their society. Trouble is brewing and danger of the dark forces is presenting itself. It’s prey, mankind and their weaknesses. From the moment they meet, Bly and Andrew are drawn to one another, helpless to resist the desire that ignites between them. Destiny has brought them together, but is it enough to overcome the obstacles that malevolent force has thrown in their path. Will the desire they share be enough to overcome the barriers of their lives that separate them?</span>
  <a data-text-id="10093668467478205055" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

      </div>

It's priceless! It is so hard to write review for book I actually like. No, it is much more - I love Elementals: Mystic Warriors. The characters in the book are so wonderful. The fact that they have supernatural abilities makes them more than just people, but the feelings they experience make them closer, because love is an absolutely eternal, unique and universal feeling and there is no more power than this. Chemistry between Bly La Croix and Andrew Von Erikson this is what intrigues and makes you want to continue their story. Excellent story! Certainly 5 stars!</span>

I tried my best to read it, but it was hard with the awkward writing. There are spelling mistakes and too long sentences that I wish would flow much better and more to the point.<br/><br/>Some examples (and this from the first 2 chapters only!)<br/>- “Some were hardened individuals that were known to be tough malicious beings...” (Possibly: Some tough malicious beings...?)<br/>- “On the whole in general some</span>
  <span id="freeText11833130708709607331" style="display:none">DNF. The premise looked interesting and promising, but unfortunately this book needs quite a lot of editing. I tried my best to read it, but it was hard with the awkward writing. There are spelling mistakes and too long sentences that I wish would flow much better and more to the point.<br /><br />Some examples (and this from the first 2 chapters only!)<br />- “Some were hardened individuals that were known to be tough malicious beings...” (Possibly: Some tough malicious beings...?)<br />- “On the whole in general some unique humans...”<br />- “Statistically speaking crime and victim related crimes was running wild” (Not sure if the author wants to make a distinction in different types of crime, but it’s not central to the story, so maybe just “crime”?)<br /><br />Anyway, if the editing doesn’t bother you, this book seems to promise riveting family secrets and magical lineages. If you enjoy that, this book might be for you.</span>

<div id="review_2877730781" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2877730781" />
    <a title="Katherine Moore" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/51581149-katherine-moore"><img alt="Katherine Moore" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1549424739p2/51581149.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2877730781?book_show_action=true">Jul 11, 2019</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Katherine Moore" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Katherine Moore" href="/user/show/51581149-katherine-moore">Katherine Moore</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span> (Review from the author)
          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/44021876-elementals">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2877730781" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7402079354973961943">Elementals Mystic Warriors is an original idea that opens a window to the world of Elementals and their influence on humanity. Powerful beings, warriors that are protectors against the malevolent forces of evil, with various gifts influenced by everything that make up this world. Guardians of man living among us yet unknown... This book covers the beginning, the origin of some and leave you wondering about others as the author subtly connects each to the other. There is friendship, family and ro</span>
  <span id="freeText7402079354973961943" style="display:none">Elementals Mystic Warriors is an original idea that opens a window to the world of Elementals and their influence on humanity. Powerful beings, warriors that are protectors against the malevolent forces of evil, with various gifts influenced by everything that make up this world. Guardians of man living among us yet unknown... This book covers the beginning, the origin of some and leave you wondering about others as the author subtly connects each to the other. There is friendship, family and romance along with the struggles they face everyday in the fight to defend mankind.<br /><br />The Von Erikson triplets are a uniquely different set of heroes. All three are billionaire entrepreneurs, movers and shakers in the world of business. The backstory of their beginning, of who they really are, could have been the makings of a book of it's own. Two brothers and a sister born of human parents but the lives of the unborn infants were affected by unforeseen circumstances of forces of evil. Andrew after centuries of waiting may have finally found his Melda quen! –Beloved One! His life mate. <br /><br />Bly La Croix, a powerful shifter, telepath and practitioner of magic. Beautiful, alluring and charming. Born into a powerful family with powers of the earth. Shifters and magic practitioners with gifts of earth's elements were her family. But she had another destiny that was unfolding, one of love and passion, that changes her life forever.<br /><br />This novel is a very good read that I put down for one day after reading it and shared with a friend to read. We are both of the same opinion that it is one that we would love to follow more of the story line when the next book comes out. Looking forward to it! </span>
  <a data-text-id="7402079354973961943" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

//<![CDATA[  

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('9MMJU1K0oU3ZKGP3uZ0Vy0YvE9S3Jz0vX5xSyYZk8GRyO66Mkvz/k7WCsbFviRmFtudwURX1pejyBIE9OrVn7g==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('JLsEVSO/i9qbGhH/lMm055TnSTro5dDp+laWD6YnUnqiQ6OK4/fVBPeww7lC3bipZC8qv0o3SC5XzkX7GvbF8A==')})
  }
//]]>

<div class='bookAuthorProfile__about'>

<span id="freeTextContainer10394054453154927705">Katherine Moore, author of Elementals Mystic Warriors, the first book of her Mystic Warriors series, lives in Houston, Texas. She is a native of Louisiana, which is where the basis for her love of reading and writing began. She has a Bachelor of Science degree from the University of Houston-Downtown. She is a mother, business owner and a former educator. While in her role as an educator she helped</span>
  <span id="freeText10394054453154927705" style="display:none">Katherine Moore, author of Elementals Mystic Warriors, the first book of her Mystic Warriors series, lives in Houston, Texas. She is a native of Louisiana, which is where the basis for her love of reading and writing began. She has a Bachelor of Science degree from the University of Houston-Downtown. She is a mother, business owner and a former educator. While in her role as an educator she helped spread her love for reading and writing to expand the minds of the students she taught.<br />Coming from a large family of eleven children, reading and writing gave her a way to have a space that she didn’t have to share. She tells friends and family that she writes for herself because it gives her a sense of freedom. With this freedom comes the ability to create characters and settings that are not locked into any one realm or reality. When she writes she becomes a part of her characters. They exist in the domain, time and space that she creates. The fact that she has the capability of presenting her characters, that create pictures and emotions that stimulate the mind is an ability that she feels blessed to have. “I love storytelling… paranormal-romance filled with action, sometimes conflicting personalities and intrigue is what I present…”, says Katherine Moore. She attributes the love of her preferred genre of writing to the stories and legends handed down from the elders that surrounded her in her youth.<br /></span>
